         // Fix any fields before converting to settings
         preset.bias_preset_selected = preset.bias_presets !== undefined ? preset.bias_preset_selected : undefined;  // presets might have bias_preset_selected but not bias_presets, but settings need both or neither.
 
         // Convert from preset to ChatCompletionSettings
         const settings = structuredClone(oai_settings);
         for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(preset)) {
             const settingToUpdate = settingsToUpdate[key];
             if (!settingToUpdate) continue;
             settings[settingToUpdate[1]] = value;
         }
 
         // Ensure api-url is properly applied for all sources that accept it

presetToGeneratePayload(preset, overridePreset = {}, overridePayload = {}) {
         if (!preset || typeof preset !== 'object') {
             throw new Error('Invalid preset: must be an object');
         }
 
         // apply preset overrides
         preset = { ...preset, ...overridePreset };
 
         // Fix any fields before converting to settings
         preset.bias_preset_selected = preset.bias_presets !== undefined ? preset.bias_preset_selected : undefined;  // presets might have bias_preset_selected but not bias_presets, but settings need both or neither.
 
         // Convert from preset to ChatCompletionSettings
         const settings = structuredClone(oai_settings);
         for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(preset)) {
             const settingToUpdate = settingsToUpdate[key];
             if (!settingToUpdate) continue;
             settings[settingToUpdate[1]] = value;
         }

         // apply preset overrides

         // Fix any fields before converting to settings
         preset.bias_preset_selected = preset.bias_presets !== undefined ? preset.bias_preset_selected : undefined;  // presets might have bias_preset_selected but not bias_presets, but settings need both or neither.

         if (!preset || typeof preset !== 'object') {
             throw new Error('Invalid preset: must be an object');
         }
 
         // apply preset overrides
         preset = { ...preset, ...overridePreset };
 
         // Fix any fields before converting to settings
         preset.bias_preset_selected = preset.bias_presets !== undefined ? preset.bias_preset_selected : undefined;  // presets might have bias_preset_selected but not bias_presets, but settings need both or neither.
 
         // Convert from preset to ChatCompletionSettings
         const settings = structuredClone(oai_settings);
         for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(preset)) {
             const settingToUpdate = settingsToUpdate[key];
             if (!settingToUpdate) continue;
             settings[settingToUpdate[1]] = value;
         }

         if (!preset || typeof preset !== 'object') {
             throw new Error('Invalid preset: must be an object');
         }
 
         // apply preset overrides
         preset = { ...preset, ...overridePreset };
 
         // Fix any fields before converting to settings
         preset.bias_preset_selected = preset.bias_presets !== undefined ? preset.bias_preset_selected : undefined;  // presets might have bias_preset_selected but not bias_presets, but settings need both or neither.
 
         // Convert from preset to ChatCompletionSettings
         const settings = structuredClone(oai_settings);
         for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(preset)) {
             const settingToUpdate = settingsToUpdate[key];
             if (!settingToUpdate) continue;
             settings[settingToUpdate[1]] = value;
         }

presetToGeneratePayload(preset, overridePreset = {}, overridePayload = {}) {
         if (!preset || typeof preset !== 'object') {
             throw new Error('Invalid preset: must be an object');
         }
 
         // apply preset overrides
         preset = { ...preset, ...overridePreset };
 
         // Fix any fields before converting to settings
         preset.bias_preset_selected = preset.bias_presets !== undefined ? preset.bias_preset_selected : undefined;  // presets might have bias_preset_selected but not bias_presets, but settings need both or neither.
 
         // Convert from preset to ChatCompletionSettings
         const settings = structuredClone(oai_settings);
         for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(preset)) {
             const settingToUpdate = settingsToUpdate[key];
             if (!settingToUpdate) continue;
             settings[settingToUpdate[1]] = value;
         }
 
         // Ensure api-url is properly applied for all sources that accept it
         ['custom_url', 'vertexai_region', 'zai_endpoint', 'siliconflow_endpoint', 'minimax_endpoint'].forEach(field => {…}processRequest: ƒ async processRequest(requestData, options, extractData = true, signal = null)prototype: {}sendRequest: ƒ async sendRequest(data, extractData = true, signal = null)arguments: (...)caller: (...)[[FunctionLocation]]: custom-request.js:421[[Prototype]]: ƒ ()[[Scopes]]: Scopes[3]EventSourceStream: class EventSourceStreamTextCompletionService: class TextCompletionServicecreateGenerationParameters: async ƒ createGenerationParameters(settings, model, type, messages, { jsonSchema = null } = {})createTextGenGenerationData: ƒ createTextGenGenerationData(settings, model, finalPrompt = null, maxTokens = null, isImpersonate = false, isContinue = false, cfgValues = null, type = 'quiet')extractJsonFromData: ƒ extractJsonFromData(data, { mainApi = null, chatCompletionSource = null, returnInvalidJson = false } = {})extractMessageFromData: ƒ extractMessageFromData(data, activeApi = null)extractReasoningFromData: ƒ extractReasoningFromData(data, {

presetToGeneratePayload(preset, overridePreset = {}, overridePayload = {}) {
         if (!preset || typeof preset !== 'object') {
             throw new Error('Invalid preset: must be an object');
         }
 
         // apply preset overrides
         preset = { ...preset, ...overridePreset };
 
         // Fix any fields before converting to settings
         preset.bias_preset_selected = preset.bias_presets !== undefined ? preset.bias_preset_selected : undefined;  // presets might have bias_preset_selected but not bias_presets, but settings need both or neither.
 
         // Convert from preset to ChatCompletionSettings
         const settings = structuredClone(oai_settings);
         for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(preset)) {
             const settingToUpdate = settingsToUpdate[key];
             if (!settingToUpdate) continue;
             settings[settingToUpdate[1]] = value;
         }
 
         // Ensure api-url is properly applied for all sources that accept it
         ['custom_url', 'vertexai_region', 'zai_endpoint', 'siliconflow_endpoint', 'minimax_endpoint'].forEach(field => {…}processRequest: ƒ async processRequest(requestData, options, extractData = true, signal = null)prototype: {}sendRequest: ƒ async sendRequest(data, extractData = true, signal = null)arguments: (...)caller: (...)[[FunctionLocation]]: custom-request.js:421[[Prototype]]: ƒ ()[[Scopes]]: Scopes[3]EventSourceStream: class EventSourceStreamTextCompletionService: class TextCompletionServicecreateGenerationParameters: async ƒ createGenerationParameters(settings, model, type, messages, { jsonSchema = null } = {})createTextGenGenerationData: ƒ createTextGenGenerationData(settings, model, finalPrompt = null, maxTokens = null, isImpersonate = false, isContinue = false, cfgValues = null, type = 'quiet')extractJsonFromData: ƒ extractJsonFromData(data, { mainApi = null, chatCompletionSource = null, returnInvalidJson = false } = {})extractMessageFromData: ƒ extractMessageFromData(data, activeApi = null)extractReasoningFromData: ƒ extractReasoningFromData(data, {

presetToGeneratePayload(preset, overridePreset = {}, overridePayload = {}) {
         if (!preset || typeof preset !== 'object') {
             throw new Error('Invalid preset: must be an object');
         }
 
         // apply preset overrides
         preset = { ...preset, ...overridePreset };
 
         // Fix any fields before converting to settings
         preset.bias_preset_selected = preset.bias_presets !== undefined ? preset.bias_preset_selected : undefined;  // presets might have bias_preset_selected but not bias_presets, but settings need both or neither.
 
         // Convert from preset to ChatCompletionSettings
         const settings = structuredClone(oai_settings);
         for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(preset)) {
             const settingToUpdate = settingsToUpdate[key];
             if (!settingToUpdate) continue;
             settings[settingToUpdate[1]] = value;
         }
 
         // Ensure api-url is properly applied for all sources that accept it
         ['custom_url', 'vertexai_region', 'zai_endpoint', 'siliconflow_endpoint', 'minimax_endpoint'].forEach(field => {…}processRequest: ƒ async processRequest(requestData, options, extractData = true, signal = null)prototype: {}sendRequest: ƒ async sendRequest(data, extractData = true, signal = null)arguments: (...)caller: (...)[[FunctionLocation]]: custom-request.js:421[[Prototype]]: ƒ ()[[Scopes]]: Scopes[3]EventSourceStream: class EventSourceStreamTextCompletionService: class TextCompletionServicecreateGenerationParameters: async ƒ createGenerationParameters(settings, model, type, messages, { jsonSchema = null } = {})createTextGenGenerationData: ƒ createTextGenGenerationData(settings, model, finalPrompt = null, maxTokens = null, isImpersonate = false, isContinue = false, cfgValues = null, type = 'quiet')extractJsonFromData: ƒ extractJsonFromData(data, { mainApi = null, chatCompletionSource = null, returnInvalidJson = false } = {})extractMessageFromData: ƒ extractMessageFromData(data, activeApi = null)extractReasoningFromData: ƒ extractReasoningFromData(data, {

presetToGeneratePayload(preset, overridePreset = {}, overridePayload = {}) {
         if (!preset || typeof preset !== 'object') {
             throw new Error('Invalid preset: must be an object');
         }
 
         // apply preset overrides
         preset = { ...preset, ...overridePreset };
 
         // Fix any fields before converting to settings
         preset.bias_preset_selected = preset.bias_presets !== undefined ? preset.bias_preset_selected : undefined;  // presets might have bias_preset_selected but not bias_presets, but settings need both or neither.
 
         // Convert from preset to ChatCompletionSettings
         const settings = structuredClone(oai_settings);
         for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(preset)) {
             const settingToUpdate = settingsToUpdate[key];
             if (!settingToUpdate) continue;
             settings[settingToUpdate[1]] = value;
         }
 
         // Ensure api-url is properly applied for all sources that accept it
         ['custom_url', 'vertexai_region', 'zai_endpoint', 'siliconflow_endpoint', 'minimax_endpoint'].forEach(field => {…}processRequest: ƒ async processRequest(requestData, options, extractData = true, signal = null)prototype: {}sendRequest: ƒ async sendRequest(data, extractData = true, signal = null)arguments: (...)caller: (...)[[FunctionLocation]]: custom-request.js:421[[Prototype]]: ƒ ()[[Scopes]]: Scopes[3]EventSourceStream: class EventSourceStreamTextCompletionService: class TextCompletionServicecreateGenerationParameters: async ƒ createGenerationParameters(settings, model, type, messages, { jsonSchema = null } = {})createTextGenGenerationData: ƒ createTextGenGenerationData(settings, model, finalPrompt = null, maxTokens = null, isImpersonate = false, isContinue = false, cfgValues = null, type = 'quiet')extractJsonFromData: ƒ extractJsonFromData(data, { mainApi = null, chatCompletionSource = null, returnInvalidJson = false } = {})extractMessageFromData: ƒ extractMessageFromData(data, activeApi = null)extractReasoningFromData: ƒ extractReasoningFromData(data, {
